b'\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x9b\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6 | In observance of Fire Prevention Month, employees of PELCO III from both Main Office and Apalit Area Office actively participated in a comprehensive fire and earthquake drill, alongside a safety awareness seminar facilitated by the Bureau of Fire Protection (BFP) Apalit BFP R3 Apalit Fire Station .\n\nThe seminar aimed to equip PELCO III employees with essential knowledge and practical skills to respond effectively to emergencies such as fires and earthquakes.\n\n"It\'s better to have it and not need it than to need it and not have it," echoed throughout the seminar, serving as a poignant reminder of the importance of proactive measures in mitigating risks.\n\n\xf0\x9f\x9a\xa8\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xba\xf0\x9d\x97\xb2\xf0\x9d\x97\xbf\xf0\x9d\x97\xb4\xf0\x9d\x97\xb2\xf0\x9d\x97\xbb\xf0\x9d\x97\xb0\xf0\x9d\x98\x86 \xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xb6\xf0\x9d\x97\xbf\xf0\x9d\x97\xb2\xf0\x9d\x97\xb0\xf0\x9d\x98\x81\xf0\x9d\x97\xbc\xf0\x9d\x97\xbf\xf0\x9d\x98\x86\xf0\x9f\x9a\xa8\n\n\xf0\x9d\x97\x95\xf0\x9d\x97\x99\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 : 09310475410\n\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 : 09985985449\n\xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 : 09981809077\n\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9b\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f: (045) 425 0084\n\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x97 \xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6: (045) 302 7227\n\n#firepreventionmonth2024'

Can be applied to any unpaid bill months starting November 27, 2023\n\n\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xae\xf0\x9d\x97\xbf\xf0\x9d\x97\xae \xf0\x9d\x98\x80\xf0\x9d\x97\xae \xf0\x9d\x97\xba\xf0\x9d\x97\xb4\xf0\x9d\x97\xae \xf0\x9d\x97\xb5\xf0\x9d\x97\xb6\xf0\x9d\x97\xbb\xf0\x9d\x97\xb1\xf0\x9d\x97\xb6 \xf0\x9d\x97\xbd\xf0\x9d\x97\xae \xf0\x9d\x97\xbb\xf0\x9d\x97\xae\xf0\x9d\x97\xb8\xf0\x9d\x97\xae\xf0\x9d\x97\xb8\xf0\x9d\x97\xae\xf0\x9d\x97\xbd\xf0\x9d\x97\xae\xf0\x9d\x97\xb4-\xf0\x9d\x97\xbf\xf0\x9d\x97\xb2\xf0\x9d\x97\xb4\xf0\x9d\x97\xb6\xf0\x9d\x98\x80\xf0\x9d\x98\x81\xf0\x9d\x97\xb2\xf0\x9d\x97\xbf \xf0\x9d\x98\x80\xf0\x9d\x97\xae \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a\xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x94 \xf0\x9d\x9f\xae\xf0\x9d\x9f\xac\xf0\x9d\x9f\xae\xf0\x9d\x9f\xaf, \xf0\x9d\x97\xbb\xf0\x9d\x97\xae\xf0\x9d\x97\xbf\xf0\x9d\x97\xb6\xf0\x9d\x98\x81\xf0\x9d\x97\xbc \xf0\x9d\x97\xae\xf0\x9d\x97\xbb\xf0\x9d\x97\xb4 \xf0\x9d\x97\xb9\xf0\x9d\x97\xb6\xf0\x9d\x97\xbb\xf0\x9d\x97\xb8 \xf0\x9d\x97\xb8\xf0\x9d\x98\x82\xf0\x9d\x97\xbb\xf0\x9d\x97\xb4 \xf0\x9d\x97\xbd\xf0\x9d\x97\xae\xf0\x9d\x97\xae\xf0\x9d\x97\xbb\xf0\x9d\x97\xbc: https://www.facebook.com/pelco3official/posts/pfbid02dRVPiTWyfynPK2NWGo2MUN7cdnqSnHURzTfiPykGWdWezUr587EAYXJimgT5bogbl\nor visit agma.pelco3.org \xf0\x9f\x92\x9a\n\nHuwag kalimutang i-like at i-follow ang aming opisyal na Facebook page upang manatiling updated sa #PELCO3AGMA2023'

Dagooc\'s insistent efforts, including the roundtable discussion he convened in March together with several stakeholders from the finance and energy sector with the assistance of the Ways and Means Committee, his bid "bore fruit" as the Energy Regulatory Commission (ERC) promulgated Resolution No. 10 ordering the NGCP to discontinue passing-on its 3% franchise tax to consumers.\n\nAside from this, it is expected that the accompanying 12% value-added tax (VAT) of the franchise tax will also be scrapped from the electricity bill.\n\nRep. Dagooc is hopeful that this development will be beneficial to all consumers of electricity as this entails lowering down electricity costs by the next billing month from the date of the ERC order.'

b'\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c \xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xaa\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xa9\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xac:\n\nAs of May 8, 2023, Red and Yellow Alerts have been issued by NGCP due to insufficient power supply in the Luzon grid. \n\nRed Alert \n1:00PM-4:00PM\n6:00PM-8:00PM\n\nYellow alert\n4:00PM-6:00PM\n\n-\n\n\xf0\x9f\x93\x8c\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa8\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f \xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x97 \xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a (\xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x97)?\n\nAng Manual Load Dropping (MLD) ay ang proseso kung saan idini-distribute ang limitadong supply ng kuryente sa iba\'t ibang lugar at customers.\n\nDahil dito, may ilang mga lugar ang makakaranas ng pansamantalang pagkawala ng supply ng kuryente, at tinatawag itong ROTATIONAL POWER INTERRUPTION.\n\nAng NGCP o System Operator ay ang nag-aabiso sa mga DISTRIBUTION UTILITIES at Electric Cooperatives ng kakulangan ng supply ng kuryente. Ang NGCP din ang nagsasagawa ng tamang alokasyon ng supply sa mga Distribution Utilities at Cooperatives.\n\nBase sa alokasyon ng binigay ng NGCP, ang mga DU\'s tulad ng PELCO III at ang iba pang mga Cooperatives ay gumagawa ng "Rotating Power Interruption Schedule", upang\nmasiguro na ang system ay mapanatiling stable sa kabila ng limitadong supply.\n\n\xf0\x9f\x93\x8c \xf0\x9d\x97\x95\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a\xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa8\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f \xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x97 \xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a (\xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x97)?\n\nIsinasagawa ng NGCP ang sistemang ito kung mayroong kakulangan sa supply ng kuryente sa power plants. Ito ay kadalasang nangyayari sa SUMMER kung saan ay matindi ang init ng panahon o kapag may forced outage ang mga planta ng elektrisidad. Dahil sa mataas na konsumo o demand sa paggamit ng kuryente, nakakaranas ng kakulangan ng supply ang mga planta sa grid. Sa pagsasagawa ng MLD o Rotational Power Interruption, ang NGCP ang nagtatakda kung anu-ano ang mga apektadong lugar, gayundin kung kailan maibabalik ang serbisyo ng kuryente.\n\n\xf0\x9f\x93\x8c \xf0\x9d\x97\x95\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9b\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c \xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x95\xf0\x9d\x97\x94 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x96 \xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa9\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6?\n\nDahil ang kakulangan ng supply ng kuryente ay nagmumula sa Generating Companies o Planta, ang PELCO III at iba pang distribution utilities ay walang kontrol dito.\n\nAng NGCP ang nagbibigay ng update sa distribution utilities tungkol sa kondisyon sa supply ng kuryente. Sila rin ang tumutukoy sa inaasahang power demand, kaya sila rin ang nagpapasya sa power outage schedules sa mga lugar na maaapektuahan.\n\n\xf0\x9f\x93\x8c \xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xaa\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa6\xf0\x9d\x97\xac\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa0 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa9\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f \n\n\xe2\x9a\xaa\xef\xb8\x8f \xf0\x9d\x97\xaa\xf0\x9d\x97\x9b\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x98 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7  -Normal ang kondisyon sa supply ng kuryente.\n\n\xf0\x9f\x9f\xa1 \xf0\x9d\x97\xac\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xaa \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 - Ito ay tumutukoy sa kalagayan ng grid kung saan ang kabuuan ng lahat ng reserba ng kuryente ay mas mababa sa kapasidad ng pinamalaking plantang gumagana.\n\n\xf0\x9f\x94\xb4 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x97 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 - Ito ay tumutukoy sa kalagayan ng sistema kapag ang reserba ay zero na o nagkakaroon na ng kakulangan sa generation. ito ay maaaring sanhi ng maintenance shutdown ng power plants, pagbabawas ng kapasidad ng iba, o pagtaas ng pangangailangan ng mga consumers.'
b'\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1 \xf0\x9f\x92\xa1\n\n\xf0\x9f\x93\x8c\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa8\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f \xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x97 \xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a (\xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x97)?\n\nAng Manual Load Dropping (MLD) ay ang proseso kung saan idini-distribute ang limitadong supply ng kuryente sa iba\'t ibang lugar at customers.\n\nDahil dito, may ilang mga lugar ang makakaranas ng pansamantalang pagkawala ng supply ng kuryente, at tinatawag itong ROTATIONAL POWER INTERRUPTION.\n\nAng NGCP o System Operator ay ang nag-aabiso sa mga DISTRIBUTION UTILITIES at Electric Cooperatives ng kakulangan ng supply ng kuryente. Ang NGCP din ang nagsasagawa ng tamang alokasyon ng supply sa mga Distribution Utilities at Cooperatives.\n\nBase sa alokasyon ng binigay ng NGCP, ang mga DU\'s tulad ng PELCO III at ang iba pang mga Cooperatives ay gumagawa ng "Rotating Power Interruption Schedule", upang\nmasiguro na ang system ay mapanatiling stable sa kabila ng limitadong supply.\n\n\xf0\x9f\x93\x8c \xf0\x9d\x97\x95\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a\xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa8\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f \xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x97 \xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a (\xf0\x9d\x97\xa0\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x97)?\n\nIsinasagawa ng NGCP ang sistemang ito kung mayroong kakulangan sa supply ng kuryente sa power plants. Ito ay kadalasang nangyayari sa SUMMER kung saan ay matindi ang init ng panahon o kapag may forced outage ang mga planta ng elektrisidad. Dahil sa mataas na konsumo o demand sa paggamit ng kuryente, nakakaranas ng kakulangan ng supply ang mga planta sa grid. Sa pagsasagawa ng MLD o Rotational Power Interruption, ang NGCP ang nagtatakda kung anu-ano ang mga apektadong lugar, gayundin kung kailan maibabalik ang serbisyo ng kuryente.\n\n\xf0\x9f\x93\x8c \xf0\x9d\x97\x95\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9b\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c \xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\x97\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2 \xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c \xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x95\xf0\x9d\x97\x94 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1\xf0\x9d\x97\x9a \xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x9f\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x96 \xf0\x9d\x97\x96\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa2\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\x94\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa9\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6?\n\nDahil ang kakulangan ng supply ng kuryente ay nagmumula sa Generating Companies o Planta, ang PELCO III at iba pang distribution utilities ay walang kontrol dito.\n\nAng NGCP ang nagbibigay ng update sa distribution utilities tungkol sa kondisyon sa supply ng kuryente. b'\xf0\x9d\x97\x9e\xf0\x9d\x97\xa8\xf0\x9d\x97\xa5\xf0\x9d\x97\xac\xf0\x9d\x97\x98\xf0\x9d\x97\xa1-\xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\x97 \xf0\x9d\x97\xa7\xf0\x9d\x97\x9c\xf0\x9d\x97\xa3\xf0\x9d\x97\xa6 \xf0\x9f\x92\xa1\n\nBase sa datos, malaki ing epekto ng temperatura sa pagkonsumo ng kuryente. b'Power rates are likely to increase further in the coming months as the impact of higher coal and crude oil importation costs trickle down to consumers, mainly due to a weak peso that has magnified the effect of high fuel prices for power generation.\n\nIn particular, in the seven months since Russia invaded Ukraine, world coal prices have more than tripled, and now remain elevated in solidarity with crude oil and gas prices. Thus, for the Philippines, which is largely dependent on imported fossil fuels (except natural gas), the depreciation of the peso, now already by 14 percent, can be catastrophic.\n\nRead more: https://www.philstar.com/business/2022/09/27/2212430/power-rates-up-up-and-away'

This may possibly be caused by maintenance shutdown of power plants, reduced capacities of others or rising demand.\n(Ito ay tumutukoy sa kalagayan ng sistema kapag ang reserba ay zero na o nagkakaroon na ng kakulangan sa generation. ito ay maaaring sanhi ng maintenance shutdown ng power plants, pagbabawas ng kapasidad ng iba, o pagtaas ng pangangailangan ng mga consumers.)\n\n-\n\nAng Electric Cooperatives, katulad ng PELCO III ay distributor lamang ng kuryente. May mga power plant na silang gumagawa ng kuryente, upang maparating sa mga Electric Cooperatives ang kuryente mula sa power plant, dumadaan ito sa high voltage transmission grid na National Grid Corporation of the Philippines.\n\nAng NGCP bilang system operator ang nagdedeklara ng MLD o Manual Load Dropping, kung anong probinsya at oras ang apektado ng rotational power interruption.\n\nHinggil rito, ang Department of Energy Philippines ay nagbibigay ng update patungkol sa kalagayan sa supply ng kuryente sa Pilipinas.'

b'Today, August 1, is National Lineman Appreciation Day, a day set aside to recognize and thank those who labor tirelessly to keep the lights on and the power going.\n\nThere are times when our linemen are called upon to repair damage caused by Mother Nature as swiftly and efficiently as possible. Our linemen work hard to immediately restore service to the affected areas. Even when there isn\xe2\x80\x99t a crisis, they have to work in risky situations every day.\n\nTheir hard work and dedication truly deserve this special day.
